href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6207" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="6282" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6284" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6184" class="Function">le-div-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6299" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6299" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6302" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6302" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6305" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6305" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="6308" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6308" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="6311" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6313" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9611" class="Function">le-leq-neq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6328" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5130" class="Function">leq-div-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6344" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6299" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6347" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6302" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6350" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6305" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="6352" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6354" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6308" class="Bound">fᵉ</a>

<a id="le-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="6358" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6358" class="Function">le-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6368" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6370" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6371" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6371" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6374" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6377" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6379" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="6381" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6383" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6385" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6399" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6404" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6411" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6371" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6414" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6417" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6419" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6371" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6422" href="foundation.negated-equality%25E1%25B5%2589.html#760" class="Function Operator">≠ᵉ</a> <a id="6425" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6428" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6430" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1342" class="Function">le-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6436" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6371" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6439" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="6442" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6358" class="Function">le-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6452" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6452" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6455" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6455" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6458" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6458" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="6461" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6461" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="6464" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6464" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="6467" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6469" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9611" class="Function">le-leq-neq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6483" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6484" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5310" class="Function">leq-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6495" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6452" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="6498" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6455" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6501" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6458" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="6504" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6461" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="6506" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6508" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6464" class="Bound">fᵉ</a>
</pre>
### `1` divides any number

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-one-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="6552" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6552" class="Function">div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6563" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6568" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6568" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6571" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6573" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="6575" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6579" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6586" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="6589" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6568" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="6592" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="6597" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6598" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6552" class="Function">div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6609" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6609" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="6611" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6613" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6615" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6609" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="6618" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="6623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6624" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6552" class="Function">div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6635" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6635" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="6637" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6639" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6641" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2055" class="Function">right-unit-law-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6663" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6635" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>

<a id="div-is-one-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="6667" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6667" class="Function">div-is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6681" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6686" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6686" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="6689" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6689" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6692" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6694" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="6696" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6698" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6700" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6710" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6686" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="6713" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6715" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6722" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6686" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="6725" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6689" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="6728" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6667" class="Function">div-is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6742" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="6743" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="DottedPattern Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="6746" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6746" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6749" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="6755" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6757" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6552" class="Function">div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6768" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6746" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
</pre>
### `x | 1` implies `x ＝ 1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-one-div-one-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="6813" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6813" class="Function">is-one-div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6831" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6833" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6834" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6834" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6837" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6839" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="6841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6843" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6845" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6852" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6834" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6855" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="6858" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6860" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6870" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6834" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="6873" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6813" class="Function">is-one-div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6891" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6891" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6894" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6894" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="6897" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6899" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4140" class="Function">antisymmetric-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6920" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6891" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="6923" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="6926" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6894" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="6929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6930" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6552" class="Function">div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6941" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6891" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="6943" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Any number divides `0`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-zero-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="6986" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6986" class="Function">div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6998" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7003" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7003" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7006" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7008" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7010" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7014" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7021" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7003" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7024" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#848" class="InductiveConstructor">0ᵉ</a>
<a id="7027" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="7032" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7033" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6986" class="Function">div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7045" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7045" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="7047" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7049" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7051" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#848" class="InductiveConstructor">0ᵉ</a>
<a id="7054" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="7059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7060" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6986" class="Function">div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7072" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="7074" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7076" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7078" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1720" class="Function">left-zero-law-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7099" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>

<a id="div-is-zero-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="7103" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7103" class="Function">div-is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7118" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7123" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7123" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7126" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7126" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7129" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7131" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7133" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7135" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7137" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1761" class="Function">is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7148" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7126" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7151" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7153" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7160" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7123" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7163" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7126" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="7166" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7103" class="Function">div-is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7181" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7181" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7184" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="7185" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="DottedPattern InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7193" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="7199" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7201" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6986" class="Function">div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7213" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7181" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
</pre>
### `0 | x` implies `x = 0` and `x | 1` implies `x = 1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-zero-div-zero-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="7286" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7286" class="Function">is-zero-div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7306" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7308" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7309" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7309" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7314" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7316" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7318" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7320" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7327" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7335" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7309" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7338" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7340" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1761" class="Function">is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7351" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7309" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="7354" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7286" class="Function">is-zero-div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7374" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7377" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7377" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="7380" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7382" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4140" class="Function">antisymmetric-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7403" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7406" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7415" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6986" class="Function">div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7427" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7374" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="7429" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7431" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7377" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>

<a id="is-zero-is-zero-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="7435" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7435" class="Function">is-zero-is-zero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7461" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7461" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7464" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7464" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="7467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7469" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7471" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7473" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7475" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7482" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7461" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7485" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7464" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="7488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7490" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1761" class="Function">is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7501" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7461" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7504" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7506" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1761" class="Function">is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7517" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7464" class="Bound">yᵉ</a>
<a id="7520" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7435" class="Function">is-zero-is-zero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7543" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="7544" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="DottedPattern InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7552" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7552" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="7555" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7555" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7558" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="7564" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7566" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7286" class="Function">is-zero-div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7586" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7552" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="7589" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7555" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
</pre>
### Any divisor of a nonzero number is nonzero

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-nonzero-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="7653" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7653" class="Function">is-nonzero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7671" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7676" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7676" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7679" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7679" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7682" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7684" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7686" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7688" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7690" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7697" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7676" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7700" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7679" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7703" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7705" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7719" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7679" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7722" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7724" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7738" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7676" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
<a id="7741" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7653" class="Function">is-nonzero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7759" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="7760" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="DottedPattern InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7768" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7768" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7771" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7771" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="7774" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7774" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="7777" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="7783" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7785" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7774" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="7788" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7789" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7286" class="Function">is-zero-div-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7809" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7768" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7812" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7771" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="7814" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Any divisor of a number at least `1` is at least `1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="leq-one-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="7887" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7887" class="Function">leq-one-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7902" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7907" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7907" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7910" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7910" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7915" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7917" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7919" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7921" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7928" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7907" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7931" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7910" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7934" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7936" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1297" class="Function">leq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7943" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="7946" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7910" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7951" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1297" class="Function">leq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7958" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="7961" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7907" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
<a id="7964" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7887" class="Function">leq-one-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7979" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7979" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="7982" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7982" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7985" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7985" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="7988" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7988" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a> <a id="7991" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="7995" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6650" class="Function">leq-one-is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8017" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7979" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8021" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7653" class="Function">is-nonzero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8039" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7979" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8042" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7982" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8045" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7985" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="8048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8049" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6823" class="Function">is-nonzero-leq-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8071" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7982" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8074" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7988" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a><a id="8076" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### If `x < d` and `d | x`, then `x` must be `0`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-zero-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="8142" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8142" class="Function">is-zero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8157" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8161" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8162" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8162" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8165" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8165" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8168" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8170" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="8172" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8174" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8176" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1342" class="Function">le-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8182" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8165" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8185" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8162" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8190" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8197" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8162" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8200" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8165" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8203" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8205" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1761" class="Function">is-zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8216" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8165" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="8219" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8142" class="Function">is-zero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8234" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8234" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8237" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8245" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8245" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="8248" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8248" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="8251" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8253" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a>
<a id="8259" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8142" class="Function">is-zero-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8274" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8274" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8278" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8286" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8286" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="8288" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8290" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8290" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="8293" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8294" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="8300" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8301" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8309" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8309" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="8311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8313" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8313" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="8315" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8317" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8321" href="foundation-core.empty-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#927" class="Function">ex-falsoᵉ</a>
    <a id="8335" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8337" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7233" class="Function">contradiction-le-ℕᵉ</a>
      <a id="8363" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8365" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8373" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8286" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="8375" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8377" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8274" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8380" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8290" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>
      <a id="8389" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8391" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2790" class="Function">concatenate-leq-eq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8413" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8274" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
        <a id="8424" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8426" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10953" class="Function">leq-add-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="8438" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8274" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="8441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8442" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8309" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8445" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8449" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8274" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="8451" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8454" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8313" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="8456" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### If `x` divides `y` then `x` divides any multiple of `y`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-mul-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="8533" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8533" class="Function">div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8544" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8548" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8549" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8549" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8552" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8552" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8555" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8555" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8560" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="8562" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8564" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8566" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8573" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8552" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8576" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8555" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8581" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8588" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8552" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8592" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8549" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8595" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8599" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8555" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="8601" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="8603" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8533" class="Function">div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8614" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8617" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8620" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8620" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8623" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8623" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="8626" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8630" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4830" class="Function">transitive-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8648" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8651" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8620" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8655" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8658" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8662" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8620" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="8664" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8667" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="8673" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8676" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="8681" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8683" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8623" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>

<a id="div-mul-ℕ&#39;ᵉ"></a><a id="8687" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8687" class="Function">div-mul-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="8699" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8703" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8704" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8704" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8707" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8710" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8710" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8713" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8715" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="8717" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8719" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8721" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8728" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8731" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8710" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8734" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8736" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8743" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8747" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8710" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8750" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8754" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8704" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="8756" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="8758" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8687" class="Function">div-mul-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="8770" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8770" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8773" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8773" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8776" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8776" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8779" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8779" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="8782" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8786" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#837" class="Function">trᵉ</a> <a id="8790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8791" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8798" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8773" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="8800" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8803" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2953" class="Function">commutative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8822" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8770" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8825" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8776" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="8827" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8829" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8830" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8533" class="Function">div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8841" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8770" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8844" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8773" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="8847" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8776" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="8850" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8779" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="8852" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### A 3-for-2 property of division with respect to addition

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-add-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="8928" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8928" class="Function">div-add-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8939" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="9139" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9141" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4020" class="Function">right-distributive-mul-add-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="9171" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9113" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="9174" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9127" class="Bound">mᵉ</a> <a id="9177" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9097" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="9179" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9181" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="9186" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9188" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1010" class="Function">ap-add-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="9198" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9116" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="9201" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9130" class="Bound">qᵉ</a><a id="9203" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9366" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="9372" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a>
