href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10260" class="Bound">yᵉ</a>
<a id="10323" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10228" class="Function">div-right-summand-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10344" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10344" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="10347" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10347" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10350" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10350" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10353" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10353" class="Bound">H1ᵉ</a> <a id="10357" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10357" class="Bound">H2ᵉ</a> <a id="10361" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="10365" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9206" class="Function">div-left-summand-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10385" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10344" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="10388" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10350" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10391" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10347" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10394" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10353" class="Bound">H1ᵉ</a> <a id="10398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10399" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2617" class="Function">concatenate-div-eq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10421" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10357" class="Bound">H2ᵉ</a> <a id="10425" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10426" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2206" class="Function">commutative-add-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10445" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10347" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10448" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10350" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="10450" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### If `d` divides both `x` and `x + 1`, then `d ＝ 1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-one-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="10521" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10521" class="Function">is-one-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10538" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10538" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10541" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10541" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10544" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10546" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="10548" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10550" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10552" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10559" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10538" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10562" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10541" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10565" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10567" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10574" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10538" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10577" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10578" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10586" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10541" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="10588" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10590" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10592" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10602" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10538" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="10605" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10521" class="Function">is-one-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10619" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10619" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10622" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10622" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10625" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10625" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="10628" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10628" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="10631" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10633" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6813" class="Function">is-one-div-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10651" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10619" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10655" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10228" class="Function">div-right-summand-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10676" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10619" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10679" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10622" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10682" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="10685" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10625" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="10688" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10628" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="10690" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Multiplication preserves divisibility

<pre class="Agda"><a id="preserves-div-mul-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="10748" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10748" class="Function">preserves-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10769" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10774" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10774" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10777" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10777" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10780" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10780" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10783" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10785" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="10787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10789" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10791" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10798" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10777" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10801" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10780" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10804" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10806" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10813" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10814" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10774" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10817" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10821" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10777" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="10823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10826" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10774" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10829" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10833" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10780" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="10835" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10837" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="10842" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10843" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10748" class="Function">preserves-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10864" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10864" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10867" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10867" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10870" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10870" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10874" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="10880" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10880" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="10883" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10883" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="10885" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10888" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10890" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10880" class="Bound">qᵉ</a>
<a id="10893" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="10898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10899" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10748" class="Function">preserves-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10920" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10920" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10923" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10923" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10926" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10926" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10930" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="10936" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10936" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="10939" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10939" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="10941" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10944" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="10948" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10950" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="10955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10956" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4400" class="Function">associative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10975" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10936" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="10978" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10920" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10981" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10923" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="10983" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10986" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
    <a id="10993" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10995" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10997" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="11001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11002" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">_*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11007" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10923" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11009" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11012" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2953" class="Function">commutative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11031" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10936" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11034" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10920" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11036" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11039" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
      <a id="11048" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11050" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11052" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4400" class="Function">associative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11071" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10920" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11074" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10936" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11077" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10923" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11079" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11081" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
        <a id="11092" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11094" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="11098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11099" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10920" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11102" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ_</a><a id="11106" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11108" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10939" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="11110" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### Multiplication by a nonzero number reflects divisibility

<pre class="Agda"><a id="reflects-div-mul-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="11189" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11189" class="Function">reflects-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11209" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="11213" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11214" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11214" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11217" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11217" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11220" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11220" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11225" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="11227" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11229" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11231" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11245" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11214" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11248" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11250" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11257" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11258" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11214" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11261" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11265" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11217" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11267" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11269" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11270" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11214" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11273" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11277" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11220" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="11279" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11281" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11283" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11290" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11217" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11293" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11220" class="Bound">yᵉ</a>
<a id="11296" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="11301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11302" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11189" class="Function">reflects-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11322" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11322" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11325" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11325" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11328" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11328" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11331" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11331" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="11334" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11335" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="11341" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11341" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11344" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11344" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="11346" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11349" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11351" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11341" class="Bound">qᵉ</a>
<a id="11354" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="11359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11360" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11189" class="Function">reflects-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11380" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11380" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11383" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11383" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11386" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11386" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11389" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11389" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="11392" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11393" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="11399" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11399" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11402" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11402" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="11404" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11407" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="11411" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6184" class="Function">is-injective-left-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11436" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11380" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11439" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11389" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>
    <a id="11446" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11448" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11450" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="11455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11456" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4400" class="Function">associative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11475" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11380" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11478" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11399" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11481" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11383" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11483" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11486" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
      <a id="11495" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11497" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11499" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="11503" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11504" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">_*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11509" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11383" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11511" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11514" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2953" class="Function">commutative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11533" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11380" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11536" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11399" class="Bound">qᵉ</a><a id="11538" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11541" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
        <a id="11552" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11554" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11556" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4400" class="Function">associative-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11575" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11399" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="11578" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11380" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11581" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11383" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11585" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
          <a id="11598" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11600" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11402" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="11602" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### If a nonzero number `d` divides `y`, then `dx` divides `y` if and only if `x` divides the quotient `y/d`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-quotient-div-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="11730" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11730" class="Function">div-quotient-div-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11754" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="11758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11759" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11759" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11762" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11762" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11765" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11765" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11770" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="11772" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11775" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11775" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="11778" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11780" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11787" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11765" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11790" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11762" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="11792" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11794" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11796" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11810" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11765" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11813" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="11817" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11825" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11765" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11828" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11832" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11759" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11834" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11836" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11762" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11839" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11841" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11848" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11759" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11852" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11868" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11765" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11871" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11762" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11874" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11775" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="11876" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11878" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11730" class="Function">div-quotient-div-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11902" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11902" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11905" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11905" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11908" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11908" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11911" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11911" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="11914" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11914" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="11917" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11917" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="11920" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="11924" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11189" class="Function">reflects-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11944" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11908" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11947" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11902" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
    <a id="11954" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11956" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11972" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11908" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="11975" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11905" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="11978" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11911" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="11980" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="11986" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11988" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11914" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="11990" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="11996" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11998" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#837" class="Function">trᵉ</a> <a id="12002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12003" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12011" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11908" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12014" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12018" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11902" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12020" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12023" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12024" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="12029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12030" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2004" class="Function">eq-quotient-div-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="12050" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11908" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12053" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11905" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12056" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11911" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12058" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12061" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11917" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="12063" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="12066" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12066" class="Function">div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12090" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12094" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12095" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12095" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12098" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12098" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12101" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12101" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12106" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="12108" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12110" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12111" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12111" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="12114" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12116" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12123" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12101" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12126" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12098" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="12128" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12130" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="12134" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12141" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12095" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12144" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12145" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12161" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12101" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12164" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12098" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12167" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12111" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12169" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12171" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12173" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12181" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12101" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12184" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12188" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12095" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12190" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12192" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12098" class="Bound">yᵉ</a>
<a id="12195" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12066" class="Function">div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12219" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12219" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12222" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12222" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12225" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12225" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12228" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12228" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="12231" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12231" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="12234" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12238" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#837" class="Function">trᵉ</a>
    <a id="12246" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12248" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12256" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12225" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12259" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12263" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12219" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12265" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="12272" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12274" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2004" class="Function">eq-quotient-div-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="12294" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12225" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12297" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12222" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12300" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12228" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12302" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12308" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12310" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10748" class="Function">preserves-div-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12331" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12225" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12334" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12219" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12337" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12338" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12354" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12225" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12357" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12222" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="12360" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12228" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12362" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12364" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12231" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="12366" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### If `d` divides a nonzero number `x`, then the quotient `x/d` is also nonzero

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-nonzero-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="12463" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12463" class="Function">is-nonzero-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12490" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12494" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12495" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12495" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12498" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12498" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12501" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12503" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="12505" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12508" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12508" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="12511" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12513" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12520" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12495" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12523" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12498" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12527" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="12531" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12545" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12498" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12548" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12550" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12565" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12581" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12495" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12584" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12498" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12587" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12508" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12589" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12591" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12463" class="Function">is-nonzero-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12618" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12619" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12619" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="12621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12623" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12624" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.(</a><a id="12626" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12645" class="DottedPattern Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12629" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="DottedPattern Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12633" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12619" class="DottedPattern Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="12635" class="DottedPattern Symbol">)</a><a id="12636" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12639" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="12645" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12645" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12648" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="12653" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12655" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12659" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6947" class="Function">is-nonzero-left-factor-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12689" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12645" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12692" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12619" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
</pre>
### If `d` divides a number `1 ≤ x`, then `1 ≤ x/d`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="leq-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="12761" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12761" class="Function">leq-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12785" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12790" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12790" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12793" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12793" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12796" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12798" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="12800" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12803" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12803" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="12806" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12808" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12815" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12790" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12818" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12793" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12820" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12822" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12824" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="12834" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12793" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12837" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12839" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1297" class="Function">leq-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12846" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="12849" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12850" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12866" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12790" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12869" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12793" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12872" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12803" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12874" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12876" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12761" class="Function">leq-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12900" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12900" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12903" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12903" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12906" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12906" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="12909" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12909" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="12912" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12916" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7887" class="Function">leq-one-div-ℕᵉ</a>
    <a id="12935" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12937" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12953" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12900" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="12956" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12903" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="12959" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12906" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="12961" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12967" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12969" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12903" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12971" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12977" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12979" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2217" class="Function">div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12999" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12900" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="13002" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12903" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="13005" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12906" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="13007" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="13013" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13015" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12909" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="13017" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### `a/a ＝ 1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-idempotent-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="13047" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13047" class="Function">is-idempotent-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13077" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13081" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13082" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13087" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="13089" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13091" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13093" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13107" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13110" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13113" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13113" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="13116" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13118" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13125" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13128" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="13130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13132" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13134" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13144" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13145" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13161" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13164" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13082" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13167" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13113" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="13169" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13171" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13047" class="Function">is-idempotent-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13201" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13209" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13209" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="13213" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13214" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13214" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="13217" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="13220" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13220" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="13222" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13224" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13226" href="foundation-core.empty-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#927" class="Function">ex-falsoᵉ</a> <a id="13236" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13237" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13209" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="13241" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="13246" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13248" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13047" class="Function">is-idempotent-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13278" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13279" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13287" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13287" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="13289" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13291" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13291" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="13295" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13296" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13296" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="13299" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="13302" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13302" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="13304" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13306" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="13310" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7582" class="Function">is-one-is-left-unit-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13337" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13296" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="13340" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13287" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13343" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13302" class="Bound">pᵉ</a>
</pre>
### If `b` divides `a` and `c` divides `b` and `c` is nonzero, then `a/b · b/c ＝ a/c`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="simplify-mul-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="13446" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13446" class="Function">simplify-mul-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13475" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13479" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13480" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13480" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13483" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13483" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="13486" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13491" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="13493" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13495" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13497" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13511" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13514" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="13518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13519" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13519" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="13522" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13524" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13531" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13483" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="13534" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13480" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="13536" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13539" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13539" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="13542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13544" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13551" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13554" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13483" class="Bound">bᵉ</a><a id="13556" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13559" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13559" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a> <a id="13562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13564" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13571" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13574" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13480" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="13576" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13578" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="13582" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13585" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13601" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13483" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="13604" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13480" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13607" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13519" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="13609" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13611" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13615" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13616" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13632" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13635" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13483" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="13638" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13539" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="13640" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13643" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a>
  <a id="13648" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13650" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13666" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13486" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13669" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13480" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="13672" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13559" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a><a id="13674" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13737" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5705" class="Function">is-injective-right-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13763" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13716" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="13766" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13720" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a>
    <a id="13774" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13776" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15236" class="Function Operator">equational-reasoningᵉ</a>

      <a id="13833" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15345" class="Function">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="13836" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14113" class="Function">a/bᵉ</a> <a id="13841" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13845" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13846" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14159" class="Function">b/cᵉ</a> <a id="13851" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13855" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13716" class="Bound">cᵉ</a><a id="13857" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="13909" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15345" class="Function">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="13912" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14113" class="Function">a/bᵉ</a> <a id="13917" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13921" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13711" class="Bound">bᵉ</a>

      <a id="13988" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15345" class="Function">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="13991" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13706" class="Bound">aᵉ</a>
        <a id="14002" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15345" class="Function">byᵉ</a> <a id="14006" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1867" class="Function">eq-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14025" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13711" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="14028" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13706" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="14031" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13724" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>

        <a id="14063" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15345" class="Function">byᵉ</a> <a id="14067" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="14072" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14073" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1867" class="Function">eq-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14092" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13716" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="14095" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13706" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="14098" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13730" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a><a id="14100" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="14105" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14113" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14113" class="Function">a/bᵉ</a> <a id="14118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14120" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a>
  <a id="14125" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14113" class="Function">a/bᵉ</a> <a id="14130" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14132" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14148" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13711" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="14151" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13706" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="14154" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13724" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>
  <a id="14159" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14159" class="Function">b/cᵉ</a> <a id="14164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14166" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a>
  <a id="14171" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14159" class="Function">b/cᵉ</a> <a id="14176" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14178" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14194" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13716" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="14197" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13711" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="14200" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13727" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a>

### If `d | a` and `d` is nonzero, then `x | a/d` if and only if `xd | a`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="simplify-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="14337" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14337" class="Function">simplify-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14366" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="14370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14371" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14371" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="14374" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14374" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="14377" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14377" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="14380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14382" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="14384" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14388" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14402" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14374" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="14405" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14408" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14408" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="14411" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14413" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14420" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14374" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="14423" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14371" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="14425" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14427" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="14431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14432" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14439" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14377" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="14442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14443" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14459" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14374" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="14462" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14371" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="14465" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14408" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="14467" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14470" href="foundation.logical-equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2190" class="Function Operator">↔ᵉ</a> <a id="14473" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14474" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14482" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14377" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="14485" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14489" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14374" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="14491" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14493" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14371" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="14495" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="14497" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="14502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14503" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="14508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14509" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14337" class="Function">simplify-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14538" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14538" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="14542" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14542" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="14544" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14546" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14547" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14547" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="14550" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="14553" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14553" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="14555" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14558" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14560" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14547" class="Bound">uᵉ</a>
<a id="14563" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="14568" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14569" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="14574" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14575" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14337" class="Function">simplify-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14604" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14605" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14605" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="14607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14609" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14610" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14610" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="14612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14615" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14615" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="14617" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14619" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14619" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="14623" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14623" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="14625" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14628" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14628" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="14631" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="14634" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14634" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="14636" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14639" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14643" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15236" class="Function Operator">equational-reasoningᵉ</a>

  <a id="15021" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5705" class="Function">is-injective-right-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15047" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14988" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="15050" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14997" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a>

</pre>
### Suppose `H : b | a` and `K : c | b`, where `c` is nonzero. If `d` divides `b/c` then `d` divides `a/c`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="div-quotient-div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="15428" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15428" class="Function">div-quotient-div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15465" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="15469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15470" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15470" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="15473" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15473" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="15476" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15479" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="15482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15484" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="15486" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15490" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15504" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15507" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15510" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15510" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="15513" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15515" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15522" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15473" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="15525" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15470" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="15527" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15532" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15532" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="15535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15537" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15544" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15547" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15473" class="Bound">bᵉ</a><a id="15549" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15552" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15552" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a> <a id="15555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15557" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15564" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15567" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15470" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="15569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15571" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="15575" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15582" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="15585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15586" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15602" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15605" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15473" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="15608" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15532" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="15610" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15612" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="15616" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15623" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="15626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15627" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15643" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15476" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15646" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15470" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="15649" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15552" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a><a id="15651" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15653" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15428" class="Function">div-quotient-div-div-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15690" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15691" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15691" class="Bound">aᵉ</a><a id="15693" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15696" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15696" class="Bound">bᵉ</a><a id="15698" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15700" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15701" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15701" class="Bound">cᵉ</a><a id="15703" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15705" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15706" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15706" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="15708" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15710" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15710" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="15714" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15714" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="15717" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15717" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="15720" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15720" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a> <a id="15723" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15723" class="Bound">Mᵉ</a> <a id="15726" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="15730" href="foundation-core.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#837" class="Function">trᵉ</a>
    <a id="15738" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15740" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15747" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15706" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="15749" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="15755" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15757" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13446" class="Function">simplify-mul-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15786" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15710" class="Bound">nzᵉ</a> <a id="15790" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15714" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="15793" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15717" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a> <a id="15796" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15720" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a><a id="15798" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="15804" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15806" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8533" class="Function">div-mul-ℕᵉ</a>
      <a id="15823" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15825" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15841" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15696" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="15844" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15691" class="Bound">aᵉ</a> <a id="15847" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15714" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="15849" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="15857" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15859" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15706" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="15861" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="15869" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15871" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15887" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15701" class="Bound">cᵉ</a> <a id="15890" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15696" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="15893" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15717" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="15895" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="15903" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15905" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15723" class="Bound">Mᵉ</a><a id="15907" class="Symbol">))</a>

### If `x` is nonzero and `d | x`, then `x/d ＝ 1` if and only if `d ＝ x`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="15997" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15997" class="Function">is-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16020" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="16132" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15997" class="Function">is-one-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16155" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16155" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16158" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="16159" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16155" class="DottedPattern Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16162" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16162" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="16165" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16165" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="16168" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="16174" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16176" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13047" class="Function">is-idempotent-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16206" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16155" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16209" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16162" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="16212" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16165" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a>

### If `x` is nonzero and `d | x`, then `x/d ＝ x` if and only if `d ＝ 1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="compute-quotient-div-is-one-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="16507" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16507" class="Function">compute-quotient-div-is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16538" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="16542" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16543" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16543" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16546" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16543" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16573"
