<a id="16625" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16507" class="Function">compute-quotient-div-is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16656" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="16657" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="DottedPattern Function">1ᵉ</a> <a id="16660" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16660" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16664" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16664" class="Bound">uᵉ</a> <a id="16667" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="16670" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16670" class="Bound">qᵉ</a><a id="16672" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16674" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="16680" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16684" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16690" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2055" class="Function">right-unit-law-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16712" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16664" class="Bound">uᵉ</a><a id="16714" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16716" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="16719" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16670" class="Bound">qᵉ</a>

<a id="is-one-divisor-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="16723" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16723" class="Function">is-one-divisor-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16741" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="16745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16746" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16746" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16749" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16749" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16754" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="16756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16758" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16760" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16774" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16749" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16779" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16780" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16780" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="16783" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16785" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16792" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16746" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16795" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16749" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="16797" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16799" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="16803" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16819" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16746" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16822" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16749" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16825" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16780" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="16828" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="16831" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16749" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16834" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16836" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16846" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16746" class="Bound">dᵉ</a>
<a id="16849" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16723" class="Function">is-one-divisor-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16867" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16867" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="16870" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16870" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16873" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16873" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="16876" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16877" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="16878" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16870" class="DottedPattern Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16881" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="16884" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16884" class="Bound">qᵉ</a><a id="16886" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16888" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="16894" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16898" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6184" class="Function">is-injective-left-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16923" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16870" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16926" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16873" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="16929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16930" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16884" class="Bound">qᵉ</a> <a id="16933" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="16936" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16941" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16942" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2055" class="Function">right-unit-law-mul-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16964" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16870" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="16966" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### If `x` is nonzero and `d | x` is a nontrivial divisor, then `x/d < x`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="le-quotient-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="17057" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17057" class="Function">le-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17076" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="17080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17081" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17081" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17084" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17084" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17089" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="17091" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17093" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17095" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17109" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17084" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17112" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17114" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17115" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17115" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="17118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17120" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17127" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17081" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17130" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17084" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="17132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17134" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17136" href="foundation-core.negation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#599" class="Function Operator">¬ᵉ</a> <a id="17139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17140" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2042" class="Function">is-one-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17150" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17081" class="Bound">dᵉ</a><a id="17152" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17154" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="17158" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1342" class="Function">le-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17164" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17165" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17181" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17081" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17184" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17084" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17187" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17115" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17189" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17191" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17084" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="17194" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17057" class="Function">le-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17213" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17216" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17219" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17219" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17222" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="17225" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17225" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="17228" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="17232" href="foundation.type-arithmetic-empty-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6943" class="Function">map-left-unit-law-coproduct-is-emptyᵉ</a>
    <a id="17274" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17276" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17292" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17295" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17298" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="17301" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="17304" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="17306" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="17312" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17314" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1342" class="Function">le-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17320" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17321" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17337" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17340" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17343" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17345" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17347" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="17349" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="17355" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17357" href="foundation-core.negation%25E1%25B5%2589.html#657" class="Function">map-negᵉ</a> <a id="17366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17367" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16723" class="Function">is-one-divisor-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17385" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17388" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17391" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17219" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17394" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17396" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17398" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17225" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="17400" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="17406" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17408" href="elementary-number-theory.strict-inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8919" class="Function">eq-or-le-leq-ℕᵉ</a>
      <a id="17430" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17432" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1780" class="Function">quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17448" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17451" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17454" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17456" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="17464" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17466" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="17468" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="17476" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17478" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5494" class="Function">leq-quotient-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17498" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17213" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="17501" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17216" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17504" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17219" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17507" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17222" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17509" class="Symbol">))</a>
